commit a060ae99d11fa955720b28f5714caa70f2ecddbb
Author: mt1970@nyu.edu <mt1970@nyu.edu@66ffb92e-73f9-0310-93c1-f5514f145a0a>
Date:   Fri Jun 10 06:50:06 2016 +0000

    First version of a new SCORM Cloud integration for Sakai.
    
    The big ideas:
    
      * The primary entry point is the Lessons tool.  Instructors can upload
        their SCORM modules to a lesson.
    
      * Uploaded modules are processed asynchronously.  Zip files go into a
        queue, and the queue is periodically processed to complete the
        uploads to SCORM Cloud in a reliable way.
    
      * Students can access the modules from a given lesson and get sent off
        to SCORM Cloud to take a module.
    
      * A background job periodically syncs results from SCORM Cloud with

    CLASSES-1453 Display Site Info as Joinable Groups for students
    
    Terribly convoluted:
    
      * Changed the "sakai.siteinfo" tool to be visible to all users.
    
      * When generating the site portal page, work out whether the user is an instructor or not, and whether the site has any joinable groups.  Pass all of this information through in the template.
    
      * When fetching the list of tools for the Site Tab dropdown (new in Neo), apply extra filtering if the user is a student.  If there are joinable groups, change "Settings" to "Joinable Groups".  Otherwise, hide the entry..
    
      * After any page has loaded:
    
        - If the user is an instructor, find the "Settings" tool menu entry and mark it as "Hidden" (to make it look like students can't see it, even though technically they can)
    
        - If the user is a student and there are joinable groups for this site, rename "Settings" to "Joinable Groups" in the tool menu, and change the icon of the tool.
    
        - If the user is a student and there are no joinable groups, just hide the menu item.

commit 3c12982e4cf86312fb7a84c66f886b35c7105384
Author: Mark Triggs <mark@dishevelled.net>
Date:   Wed Oct 4 17:17:29 2017 +1100

    CLASSES-3027 Prevent chrome from downloading recorded wav files
    
    When previewing an announcement that contains an audio recording,
    Chrome on OSX would download the wav file in addition to showing the
    HTML5 player.  It turns out CKEditor was emitting two sets of tags: an
    <audio> tag and an <object> tag.  The <object> tag was being ignored,
    but was causing the download.
    
    Since all modern browsers now support the <audio> tag, it seems that
    we don't need the <object> one anyway.  I've removed it, and replaced
    the "player 1 of 2" "player 2 of 2" placeholders with a generic one.

Author: Mark Triggs <mark@dishevelled.net>
Date:   Tue Jul 31 12:04:30 2018 +1000

    CLASSES-3380 Support rosters with inactive students
    
    Previously, all users imported from rosters would be loaded with a
    status of "active" in the course site in question.  This commit
    changes that behavior to only activate users whose status is "active"
    in the roster.  Otherwise, they're imported as inactive.
    
    This new behavior can be disabled at runtime by setting the following
    sakai.properties entry:
    
         nyu.rosters-enable-inactive-users=false
